The house itself is a perfectly maintained period piece. The fireplace surround is made of Batchelor tiles. (Ernest A. Batchelder was an American artist and educator who made Southern California his home in the early 20th century. He is famous as a maker of art tiles and as a leader in the American Arts and Crafts Movement.). But onto Roberta and her over the top hospitality.                      <div data-reactid="1227">
                      <div data-reactid="1228">
                       Historic Greene &amp; Greene Queen Anne Cottage, close to Old Pasadena, Metro and the Rose Bowl. Spacious, 450 sq. ft private second floor room with on-suite modern bathroom and secure onsite parking.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="1229">
                       We live in a beautiful historic Greene &amp; Greene house in the Raymond/Summit Historic District very close to Old Pasadena, the Rose Bowl and many of the City's cultural destinations and shopping district. We require a minimum 2 day in advance inquiry prior to booking. Unfortunately, we will decline any attempt to make bookings under that lead time. You will access your private second floor en-suite room off the back deck. Our home is a fully restored 2-storey, 3 bedrooms, 3 bathrooms private residence. The bedroom includes a comfortable queen bed with duvet, linens, dressers and a closet. There is a mini refrigerator, microwave, kettle, coffee maker, TV, iron/board, desk/table and chairs, together with a settee; a roll-away bed is available upon request.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="1230">
                       North Summit Avenue is located in the heart of the Raymond/Summit Historic District. It is a demographically racially mixed neighborhood within walking distance of Old Pasadena shops and businesses. Pasadena is located at the base of the San Gabriel Mountains where there are plenty of trails to hike and explore. Local places to visit include the Huntington Library, the Norton Simon Museum, the Japanese American Museum, Pasadena Museum of California Art, the Pasadena Playhouse the Gamble House many of Pasadena's nationally acclaimed historic districts.
                      </div>

                     <div data-reactid="1985">
                      <div data-reactid="1986">
                       This quiet and peaceful room is in a lovely house with a shady back patio. Our neighborhood is quiet &amp; friendly, while being close to the bus &amp; train for a quick trip into old town &amp; the great restaurants of Pasadena! Breakfast is included :).
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="1987">
                       This one-person or couple private room has access to a beautiful landscaped patio backyard. There is close access to the kitchen and bath, and the neighborhood is safe and quiet. Free wifi and street parking available, and within close distance to public transportation. The house is set in a lovely tree lined neighborhood and the house is a charming 1930's-style with hardwood floors and custom molding. I have a large collection of eclectic art that I have gathered during my travels, and which you will see through out the house. Nearby attractions include Old Town Pasadena as well as the beautiful Huntington Gardens and Descanso Gardens, the Norton Simon Museum, The Pacific Asia Museum and the California Museum of Art. Pasadena is also known for its wide variety of excellent restaurants. Host is flexible and accommodating, and is happy to provide directions and information about the area. This space is also available for film shoots, at the rate of $75/hour.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="1988">
                       this is a very quiet, tree lined neighbourhood, with great neighbours. Lots of walking with dogs and chatting with people as they pass the house.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="1989">
                       <li data-reactid="1990"><p data-reactid="1991">I stayed with Carolyn while I attended a course at the Huntington Library in Pasadena. The location is great for me. Carolyn's place is about a 45 minute walk to the Huntington library, which I enjoy doing in the fresh, morning air, or about five minutes by car. It's also only a couple of minutes walk to the Gold Line station, which goes straight to downtown LA, and old town Pasadena. I love Carolyn's home. It's beautiful, clean, and comfortable. Carolyn made me feel very welcome. I really love the garden and court yard, the photos don't really show just how lovely it is. And it's a privilege to stay with a talented harpist. I was lucky to listen in on Carolyn teaching a couple of students how to play. I took advantage of the kitchen to make breakfast at home. Carolyn provides coffee, tea, milk, cereal, toast, fruit and yoghurt, and eggs. I especially love that Carolyn (as a fellow Australian) always has vegemite in stock. But don't worry, she won't make you eat it! She is also happy to let you cook other meals if you want, but I took advantage of the local restaurants. What other reviewers have said about Carolyn being a wonderful person is true. She is warm and friendly and happy to chat over a coffee or a glass of wine, but she is not a needy host and respects privacy and personal space when you feel like peace and quiet.
